Shipping
     __________________________________________________________________

What shipping methods do you use?

   We use Priority Post. We ship from EU, so with all EU customers we’ve
   got near 100% delivery rate as shipments skip customs altogether.

Do you ship outside EU?

   Yes, we ship worldwide, except US, Canada and Australia.

What if my shipment doesn't clear customs?

   This happens very rarely as shipments from EU get less attention than
   shipments from lets say India. Should your shipment be seized you’ll be
   able to choose between a full refund or a free reshipment.

How long will it take to get my package?

   Usually for orders inside EU delivery time is 3-6 working days. Orders
   outside EU take 6-8 working days to be delivered. That said we’ve had
   orders inside EU wandering for 2 weeks before delivery and some US
   orders arriving in a few days, go figure.

Payment
     __________________________________________________________________

What is Bitcoin?

   Bitcoin is a digital currency in which transactions can be done without
   the need for a third party, e.g. bank. Its a way for you to pay us
   without asking anyone’s permission.

How can I get Bitcoins?

   See our page [18]How to Buy Bitcoins >.

How will I know if you received my Bitcoins

   You will get an email about completed payment. That usually happens 20
   minutes after you send Bitcoins.

Why do you always change Bitcoin address to which I have to pay?

   Every order gets a unique Bitcoin payment address. That’s done to
   increase security and anonymity.

Do you have other payment methods besides Bitcoin?

   No, we only support Bitcoin payments.

Have any questions we didn't answer?

[33]What is Noopept?

     [34]europills   [35]September 18, 2015   [36]Blog   [37]Leave a
   comment

   Noopept (n-phenylacetyl-l-prolylglycine ethyl ester) is, in many ways,
   the nootropic to end all nootropics. Users report increased cognitive
   capacities, increased memory, increased learning ability, and improved
   verbal acuity. One individual went so far as to say,

   “Noopept […] has now spawned an incredible improvement in myself. I am
   much more confident, far more verbally acrobatic, and I am able to
   socialize and interact with people on a whole other level than I have
   in quite some time, possibly better than ever.”

Noopept Effects

     * Enhances cognition
     * Reduces anxiety
     * Boosts mood
     * Provides neuroprotection

   Research into Noopept’s mechanism of action has revealed that it works
   very differently than other racetams (and many don’t consider it a
   racetam at all). In animal studies, Noopept increased Nerve Growth
   Factor (NGF) and Brain-Derived Neurotrophic Factor (BDNF) in the
   hippocampus while the Noopept itself left the body fairly quickly. The
   animal studies did not detect any tolerance to Noopept, and there was
   some evidence that prolonged use of Noopept led to stronger effects.

Additional N-phenylacetyl-L-prolylglycine ethyl ester Benefits

   N-phenylacetyl-L-prolylglycine ethyl ester, the scientific name for
   noopept, is a new addition to several mainstream preworkout blends.

   Why would noopept, a cognitive enhancer, be a smart choice to include
   as one of your preworkout supplements? N-phenylacetyl-L-prolylglycine
   ethyl ester enhances your focus, allowing you to power through a tough
   workout.

   If your mind is wandering instead of fixating on the workout at hand,
   your results will suffer. The addition of noopept to your preworkout
   gets you past your mental hurdles to achieve maximum results in the
   gym.

                           Pramiracetam VS Noopept




   Noopept Pramiracetam
   Strength 1000x more potent than the original racetam 10-15x more potent
   than the original racetam
   Effects Boosts mood, lowers anxiety, and enhances cognition Boosts
   cognition and productivity
   Method of action Modulates AMPA receptors to increase synaptic
   plasticity leading to many cognitive benefits. Boosts the rate of
   acetylcholine synthesis to help the brain form new neurons and improve
   working memory.
   Dose 10mg 250mg


Noopept Dosage

   Known to be 1000 times more potent than the original racetam, Noopept’s
   small dosage is another point of note. While many nootropics require a
   hefty amount of powder per dose, Noopept calls for a miniscule 10mg and
   is just as effective if not more so.

   By demonstrating itself as a powerhouse brain enhancer, Noopept is a
   great addition to any morning or afternoon stack. Noopept stands as a
   leader in the field, and continues to gain fans as more people discover
   its rewards.

   As with any cognitive enhancers, it is recommended that you consult a
   health care professional before taking Noopept.

How to Buy Bitcoins

   [18]bittylicious2

   There are many places to get Bitcoins, but we recommend
   [19]Bittylicious.com, especially if you live in EU. Besides credit
   cards Bittylicious also supports SEPA payments, through which Bitcoins
   can be purchased via regular online banking in just 1-2 hours.

   The website is straightforward and doesn’t need much explanation.
   Bittylicous.com also provides a helpful [20]buying guide>.

   You will also need a wallet to store your Bitcoins. If you prefer your
   wallet to live in your computer we recommend [21]MultiBit. If you would
   like a cloud based wallet we heard good things about [22]BlockChain.

[33]Armodafinil or Modafinil – What is the Difference?

     [34]europills   [35]July 1, 2015   [36]Blog   [37]Leave a comment

   Modafinil and Armodafinil are similar smart drugs used to increase
   energy and improve concentration and alertness. Modafinil (brand name
   Provigil) was developed in 1994 to treat narcolepsy. Armodafinil (brand
   name Nuvigil) has only been introduced in 2007. Armodafinil is similar
   to Modafinil and has only slightly modified chemical structure, making
   it more potent. So which is better as a smart drug (nootropic) –
   Armodafinil or Modafinil?

   They both are used to treat same conditions and are very effective.
   While Armodafinil requires a smaller dosage, Modafinil effects may
   still be preferred by some users. Asking which is better discounts the
   fact that different drugs can have different reactions for different
   people. Potency is not the only factor, what matters more is the
   experience you receive when using a smart drug.

   Modafinil:

   For users who suffer from narcolepsy, sleep apnea, or other sleep
   problems, Modafinil was the first medication to actually provide real
   relief. The pill helps to normalize sleep and acts as a wakefulness
   agent, allowing users to go about their lives without constant fatigue.
   Modafinil is often used off label to increase energy and focus.

   Reviews from users say Modafinil gives them dramatically improved focus
   and productivity. Along with this intense focus comes an increased
   fluency or fluidity of thought. Even ordinary tasks like reading and
   writing require much less effort or attention. It is easier to make
   connections and recall memories and retention is also higher. Some
   report improved sensory perceptions and even appetite suppression.

   Armodafinil:

   Armodafinil benefits are similar to those of Modafinil. The wakefulness
   effect is very pronounced, like a dose of caffeine, but unlike caffeine
   there are no jitters or nervousness and it does not increase (nor
   decrease) blood pressure or pulse rate. Armodafinil is quite safe and
   has almost zero addictiveness (Modafinil does have a slightly higher
   potential for side effects and tolerance).

   Unlike Modafinil, Armodafinil will not disturb your sleep patterns.
   Even after using the supplement you will not have a sudden drop off and
   will be able to go to sleep the same time as normal. You will also wake
   up at your regular hours. Modafinil users say often it is impossible to
   sleep within 5-10 hours after taking a pill. In some regard this can be
   a negative if a user is looking for a drug that helps him stay awake
   for long hours.

   Armodafinil also improves focus, but it isn’t as intense as Modafinil
   for most users. This makes Armodafinil better suited for continuous use
   as opposed to Modafinil which should be cycled or used
   occasionally. Armodafinil certainly improves productivity and also
   often boosts memory and mental fluidity. It has only been available for
   a few years, but already more than 2 million prescriptions were written
   and its being taken by all types of people ranging from entrepreneurs
   to athletes, from students to shift workers.

   Armodafinil vs Modafinil:

   The difference between these two nootropics is in their chemical
   structure. Armodafinil is an enantiomer of Modafinil. This means that
   Armodafinil consist of only the (R)-enatiomer which is the active
   component of Modafinil. Modafinil has both left and right-handed
   enantiomers in its structure. Consisting of only right enantiomer
   Armodafinil is basically a purified version of Modafinil. Consequently,
   it binds differently to receptor sites within the brain and body. While
   Modafinil dosage is 200mg, only 150mg of Armodafinil are needed to get
   the same effect.

   There are differences between how these drugs will affect you, but most
   differences are dependent on the person who is actually taking the
   drugs. Some reviews say that Modafinil has a bigger mood enhancement
   effect, improving confidence and drive. Same users find that
   Armodafinil makes them feel a little edgy and a bit aggressive. These
   difference are not expressed for everyone and should be taken as an
   indication of where differences might be noticed.

   Important issue to consider is tolerance. While many people have taken
   these drugs for a long period of time without any noticeable drop off
   in effects, others observed that tolerance can build quite quickly.
   Tolerance also seems to be more associated with Modafinil than
   Armodafinil. This can be overcome by cycling or only using Modafinil on
   occasion.

   http://eupillu4np223oxe.onion/?p=8146 Modafinil is a drug that promotes
   wakefulness, it&#8217;sapproved by the FDA as a safe alternative to
   otherstimulants. It also helps with narcolepsy, shift work sleep
   disorder and daytime fatigue that is causedby sleep apnea. Modafinil is
   also usedoff-label in the treatment of ADHD and as a nootropicor smart
   drug. Even though there has been extensive <p>Modafinil is a drug that
   promotes wakefulness, it&#8217;sapproved by the FDA as a safe
   alternative to otherstimulants. It also helps with narcolepsy, shift
   work sleep disorder and daytime fatigue that is causedby sleep apnea.
   Modafinil is also usedoff-label in the treatment of ADHD and as a
   nootropicor smart drug. Even though there has been extensive research
   the precise mechanisms of action is stillunclear. Howeverwe do have an
   understanding of how Modafinilworks in general.</p> <p
   class="p1"><strong>How does Modafinilwork?</strong></p> <p
   class="p1">Modafinilhelps to elevate levels of hypothalamic histamine.
   Researchers found this to be a wakefulness-promoting agent, compared to
   the other amphetamine type stimulants on the market.</p> <p
   class="p1">Modafinilhas the ability to inhibit many of the actions of
   the dopamine transporter. This leads to a boost in extracellular, and
   thus, synaptic concentrations of dopamine.</p> <p class="p1">One of the
   considered mechanisms of action involves orexins, which are brain
   peptides. Orexin neurons can be found within the hypothalamus, but also
   projects to several different parts of the brain, including many areas
   that can regulate wakefulness in the body.</p> <p>Activating these
   neurons will help to increase the dopamine and norepinephrine levels in
   those areas, and increases histamine levels in the histaminergic
   neurons. Studies involving rats have shown that Modafinilincreases the
   histamine release levels in the brain, which can be a possible
   mechanism of action in humans as well.</p> <p>Orexin receptors 1 and 2
   are the two orexin receptors in the body. Animals that have defective
   orexin systems showsymptoms that are similar to narcolepsy. Modafinil
   appears to activate these orexin neurons in the animal models, and they
   helpto promote wakefulness.</p> <p class="p1"><strong>ModafinilBenefits
   and Dosages</strong></p> <p class="p1">Typically the prescribed dosage
   is one 200 mg pill perday. However most users start at 100mg if their
   goal is to use Modafinil as a smart drug and not as a treatment to any
   particular health condition.</p> <p class="p1">For conditions that
   arent shift work related, Modafinilis usuallytaken during the morning
   hours.Taking Modafinillater in the day can make it difficult to fall
   asleep at night.</p> <p>Modafinil was also shown to be an effective
   treatment forADHD.</p>

   http://eupillu4np223oxe.onion/armodafinil-or-modafinil-what-is-the-diff

   http://eupillu4np223oxe.onion/armodafinil-or-modafinil-what-is-the-diff
   erence/#respond Wed, 01 Jul 2015 11:18:10 +0000 europills Blog
   http://eupillu4np223oxe.onion/?p=8127 Modafinil and Armodafinil are
   similar smart drugs used to increase energy and improve concentration
   and alertness. Modafinil (brand name Provigil) was developed in 1994 to
   treat narcolepsy.Armodafinil (brand name Nuvigil) has only been
   introduced in 2007. Armodafinil is similar to Modafinil and has only
   slightly modified chemical structure, making it more potent. So which
   is <p>Modafinil and Armodafinil are similar smart drugs used to
   increase energy and improve concentration and alertness. Modafinil
   (brand name Provigil) was developed in 1994 to treat
   narcolepsy.Armodafinil (brand name Nuvigil) has only been introduced in
   2007. Armodafinil is similar to Modafinil and has only slightly
   modified chemical structure, making it more potent. So which is better
   as a smart drug (nootropic)  Armodafinil or Modafinil?</p> <p>They both
   are used to treat same conditions and are very effective. While
   Armodafinil requires a smaller dosage, Modafinil effects may still be
   preferred by some users. Asking which is better discounts the fact that
   different drugs can have different reactions for different people.
   Potency is not the only factor, what matters more is the experience you
   receive when using a smart drug.</p> <p
   class="p1"><strong>Modafinil:</strong></p> <p class="p1">For users who
   suffer from narcolepsy, sleep apnea, or other sleep problems, Modafinil
   was the first medication to actually provide real relief. The pill
   helps to normalize sleep and acts as a wakefulness agent, allowing
   users to go about their lives without constant fatigue. Modafinil is
   often used off label to increase energy and focus.</p> <p
   class="p1">Reviews from users say Modafinil gives them dramatically
   improved focus and productivity. Along with this intense focus comes an
   increased fluency or fluidity of thought. Even ordinary tasks like
   reading and writing require much less effort or attention. It is easier
   to make connections and recall memories and retention is also higher.
   Some report improved sensory perceptions and even appetite
   suppression.</p> <p class="p1"><strong>Armodafinil:</strong></p> <p
   class="p1">Armodafinil benefits are similar to those of Modafinil. The
   wakefulness effect is very pronounced, like a dose of caffeine, but
   unlike caffeine there are no jitters or nervousness and it does not
   increase (nor decrease) blood pressure or pulse rate. Armodafinil is
   quite safe and has almost zero addictiveness (Modafinil does have a
   slightly higher potential for side effects and tolerance).</p> <p
   class="p1">Unlike Modafinil, Armodafinil will not disturb your sleep
   patterns. Even after using the supplement you will not have a sudden
   drop off and will be able to go to sleep the same time as normal. You
   will also wake up at your regular hours. Modafinil users say often it
   is impossible to sleep within 5-10 hours after taking a pill. In some
   regard this can be a negative if a user is looking for a drug that
   helps him stay awake for long hours.</p> <p class="p1">Armodafinilalso
   improves focus, but it isn&#8217;t as intense as Modafinil for most
   users. This makes Armodafinil better suited for continuous use as
   opposed to Modafinil which should be cycled or used
   occasionally.Armodafinil certainly improves productivity and also often
   boosts memory and mental fluidity. It has only been available for a few
   years, but already more than 2 million prescriptions were written and
   its being taken by all types of people ranging from entrepreneurs to
   athletes, from students to shift workers.</p> <p
   class="p1"><strong>Armodafinil vs Modafinil:</strong></p> <p
   class="p1">The difference between these two nootropics is in their
   chemical structure. Armodafinil is an enantiomer of Modafinil. This
   means that Armodafinil consist of only the (R)-enatiomer which is the
   active component of Modafinil. Modafinil has both left and right-handed
   enantiomers in its structure. Consisting of only right enantiomer
   Armodafinil is basically a purified version of Modafinil. Consequently,
   it binds differently to receptor sites within the brain and body. While
   Modafinil dosage is 200mg, only 150mg of Armodafinil are needed to get
   the same effect.</p> <p class="p1">There are differences between how
   these drugs will affect you, but most differences are dependent on the
   person who is actually taking the drugs. Some reviews say that
   Modafinil has a bigger mood enhancement effect, improving confidence
   and drive. Same users find that Armodafinil makes them feel a little
   edgy and a bit aggressive. These difference are not expressed for
   everyone and should be taken as an indication of where differences
   might be noticed.</p> <p class="p1">Important issue to consider is
   tolerance. While many people have taken these drugs for a long period
   of time without any noticeable drop off in effects, others observed
   that tolerance can build quite quickly. Tolerance also seems to be more
   associated with Modafinil than Armodafinil. This can be overcome by
   cycling or only using Modafinil on occasion.</p>
   http://eupillu4np223oxe.onion/armodafinil-or-modafinil-what-is-the-diff
   erence/feed/ 0

[34]How Does Modafinil Work?

     [35]europills   [36]July 1, 2015   [37]Blog   [38]Leave a comment

   Modafinil is a drug that promotes wakefulness, it’s approved by the FDA
   as a safe alternative to other stimulants. It also helps with
   narcolepsy, shift work sleep disorder and daytime fatigue that is
   caused by sleep apnea. Modafinil is also used off-label in the
   treatment of ADHD and as a nootropic or smart drug. Even though there
   has been extensive research the precise mechanisms of action is
   still unclear. However we do have an understanding of how
   Modafinil works in general.

   How does Modafinil work?

   Modafinil helps to elevate levels of hypothalamic histamine.
   Researchers found this to be a wakefulness-promoting agent, compared to
   the other amphetamine type stimulants on the market.

   Modafinil has the ability to inhibit many of the actions of the
   dopamine transporter. This leads to a boost in extracellular, and thus,
   synaptic concentrations of dopamine.

   One of the considered mechanisms of action involves orexins, which are
   brain peptides. Orexin neurons can be found within the hypothalamus,
   but also projects to several different parts of the brain, including
   many areas that can regulate wakefulness in the body.

   Activating these neurons will help to increase the dopamine and
   norepinephrine levels in those areas, and increases histamine levels in
   the histaminergic neurons. Studies involving rats have shown that
   Modafinil increases the histamine release levels in the brain, which
   can be a possible mechanism of action in humans as well.

   Orexin receptors 1 and 2 are the two orexin receptors in the body.
   Animals that have defective orexin systems show symptoms that are
   similar to narcolepsy. Modafinil appears to activate these orexin
   neurons in the animal models, and they help to promote wakefulness.

   Modafinil Benefits and Dosages

   Typically the prescribed dosage is one 200 mg pill per day. However
   most users start at 100mg if their goal is to use Modafinil as a smart
   drug and not as a treatment to any particular health condition.

   For conditions that aren’t shift work related, Modafinil is
   usually taken during the morning hours. Taking Modafinil later in the
   day can make it difficult to fall asleep at night.

   Modafinil was also shown to be an effective treatment for ADHD.
   [39]Armodafinil or Modafinil – What is the Difference?
